<Review>Jim and Eric are absolutely the best! I've gone to Wilson's, BoomBotz, Staygold, patio barber, Rick's, DTR, and a handful of others. I have lived literally a 2 minute walk away from Mike&Jim's for the better part of a decade and I missed out on them for a few years while I chased the trendy revivals of the "old school" barber shops. I've met some great barbers in my hunt, but honestly once you get past the too cool for school attitudes, up and covers still learning the ropes, and barber babes, sometimes it's just nice to get to a real life family buisness where machismo and ego are nonexistent and you just get great father and son team you have prefect and handed down the craft. When I say these guys are great, I mean I was taking about my wedding I was getting ready for and Jim tells me this cuts a wedding gift! < Review>
The staff is very friendly and very patient. My family and I arrived to complete the passport process per our appointment times. There was one woman who arrived 15 minutes past her appointment time and seemed to expect to jump ahead of everyone else who arrived on-time. The supervisor calmly and professionally advised the woman she arrived late and would either have to reschedule or wait until all appointments cleared for further assistance. The woman eventually stormed off, and the supervisor kindly continued to assist my family and I. Several customers appeared to take out their frustrations on the staff, but it appeared such customers failed to prepare for their appointment or review all passport requirements on the library website. When completing the process, arrive early. Have checks or money orders ready and all documents available including ID's to avoid wasting anyone's time including yours. The process may take a little longer than 15 minutes, but the staff work diligently to get the process completed in a timely manner.< /Review>

< Text>
Library's are great.  This one is no exception.    It offers lots of options,   it has its basic set up, Adult section and kids sections.  I just started taking my little girl there.  She loves books.  loves it when me and the wife read to her.  She loved looking at the pictures.   In this digital age it's nice to still have something analog that you can hold as a  physical item.    They do have computers there in the kids section that my girl loves to play on.  nice educational programs.   This is not the main reason I bring her here.  She actually has fun picking out what she may like.  I also take her to the used books for sale section.  They are a steal!. The most expensive only being about $1.   But basically, library's are good.</Text>

This library used to be a very well kept, staffed library. But that was about 2 years ago. I live near it and stop by to study about 4 days a week. Now it's just plain awful. The WI-FI was not working yesterday so I thought OK it will be back on by tomorrow, nope! Just left and it is still down! This is one of many things wrong with this library. The bathrooms are always closed / dirty so people get directed to another smaller one strictly for handicapped people! Half of the parking lot was closed well over a year and construction went over by several months when it was supposed to be open, homeless people always sleeping in chairs and staff says and does nothing! All these constant problems!!!!!!!!!! STAY AWAY IF YOU ARE WISE!!!!!!! I am now going to the National City library as I am tired of the constant problems this library has!!!!!!!!< /Text>

<time>1549757539582</time><Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
The main branch location is an extremely resourceful place to check out books, movies, certain tools and devices for those with a library card. Also to do homework, go online, hang out with library buddies, learn, read, study, and to wonder. Wonder just how in the world would life be without no actual books to hold in your hand to feel, to look at, and to touch as you turn the pages. The layout of the library is easy to navigate with high vaulted ceilings in the main adult sections for a spacious area that is naturally illuminated quite well on the sunniest days. The childrens section is quite sizeable too. With a selection that is abound with reading material that should satisfy most young avid readers palette. Plenty of chairs, tables, and seats to situate yourself for any of the activities listed above. It has undergone several refurbishments throughout the years and could use some touch ups here and there. Otherwise it is a fantastic place to immerse yourself in everything what a library offers;) Attentive, helpful, and wonderful librarian staff are never too far away to assist you. Thank you Alan and Erni for my library card!<//text>

<user_name>vitatea</user_name>< Gmap_id>
0x80c2bb24409dec3b:0xb5f2e5e045bab520<//Gmap_id>
< text>
After reading reviews on yelp, I was skeptical to order from here. However, I asked my friend about her experience and decided to go for it after she explained how great the eternal roses were as gifts and how they never came damaged in any way. Fast forward to when my eternal rose that I ordered for mother's day arrived. I was a bit shocked at the packaging it came in. It was laying on its side in the box with only bubble wrap surrounding it. If I'm paying this much for a rose, I at least expect it to be placed in a specialized box that lets the rose sit up-right. There were also two noticeable rips on the center petals. I understand roses tend to have natural tears, but these were not natural. One looked like a chunk of the petal was about to fall off. I would have let it go if the rips were on less noticeable petals. When I contacted customer service, the woman kept repeating that the rips looked "nothing-out-of-the-ordinary" and that these are real roses, not plastic. As if I didn't know what I ordered. She couldn't rectify the issue because apparently these rips were normal. After telling my friend what happened, she was also appalled by the service I received and was disappointed that I didn't get the same quality of roses that she would always get. She urged me to contact another person. When I did, I was again denied any solution. I was given the exact same template answers. "These are real roses, not plastic." Yes I know what real roses look like and they never have such serious rips. I was thrown off by the poor customer service more so than the actual rose. I recommend just getting real ones from J'Adore Les Fleurs.<//text>

<Rating>4< /Rating>< Review>
I went in the day of Christmas Eve and was seen promptly. The doctor who saw me diagnosed a chest virus but did prescribe antibiotics and OTC cough syrup. I am visiting from Hawaii and visiting friends so you can understand my misery! I went back to my friends house and curled up in bed and hibernated in their guest room until New Years Eve when I decided I was either dying or I wished I was!

On going back in to the clinic with severe, and obvious, pulmonary distress I was advised to take a seat in the full waiting room. I politely told the desk clerk I was having difficulty breathing and I was informed it was first come first served. After listening to me try to breath (no joke I could NOT breath!) my friend, who had driven me because she didn't trust me to drive as I was, went to the counter and rather coldly told the clerk I could not breathe and I needed to be seen NOW!

I was seen almost immediately after that, lol. The doctor looked at my BP, oxygen levels, and chest sounds (around my coughing fits that left me limp and dizzy) and immediately told me I needed to be seen in the ER and I needed an ambulance and an oxygen bottle. My friend said that was good and she would meet me there. They called the ambulance and stayed with me until they arrived, giving me a breathing treatment while we waited. Turns out I had double pneumonia!

So, to recap, I received excellent service from the doctors and medical personnel. The clerks were polite but rather uncaring on the 2nd visit. Just a recommendation,  if someone says they can't breath BELIEVE them!! Otherwise, I do recommend this location.</Review>

This place is pho-king amazing! Their broth tasted so clean as if there was no MSG (Dont know if it's true and don't want to know). It was probably one of the few Briggs I've had with pho that tasted so good that I didn't even have to add any sauces for extra flavor. I ordered their rib eye pho and it definitely hit the spot, especially since I've been sick; pho makes everything better. At any pho spots, I always ask for extra cilantro because cilantro goes with everything and I can never get enough of it.
They also give you a lot of meat with your noodles, which by the way, you can order with fat or skinny (I believe that's what they called it) rice noodles. Try it with the fat/flat noodles next time because it makes a difference, in my opinion.< /review>

<resp>None< /resp><rate>5< /rate><gmapID>0x80dd287d7bd4e4d9:0x6ac992fe2a792409< /gmapID>< name>

<user>102723251077111914625</user><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNAW5ISKbkTYBBhZZm0ImgvsC1GRYcSCUp9k57s=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOcQrQqCtRKoWzp8SX6nWpCYiiqSTu0h3tCdQ2l=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures><Review>I've eaten at my fair share of pho restaurants in San Diego county, but this was my first try in Orange County. A local friend told me about a place that used filet mignon,made fresh noodles, and had the best broth. That place was Pho 45. And he wasn't exaggerating.

From the outside, it's just another unassuming store front in Little Saigon. When you walk inside, it's still your typical little Asian restaurant with crowded booths and (beautiful) hand-painted bamboo decor on the walls. Service was fine, though the wait staff must have confused us with regulars because he asked us if we were ready to order before we even looked at the menu.

We started with a few couple appetizer staples: spring rolls with peanut sauce, and egg rolls with fish sauce. The spring rolls tasted freshly made and the fried egg rolls were also tasty. I decided to order the large combination pho bowl, and I wasn't disappointed. I took a sip of the broth and it had a rich, hearty flavor. The noodles were delicious, the steak was tender, and just a hint of saute added just the right kick. The large was surprisingly filling. My wife couldn't even finish the small.

Pricing was average for pho, but the quality was top notch. Overall, if you're looking for the best bowl of pho in OC (and maybe all of SoCal) don't hesitate to stop here!<//Review></record></dataset><record>

<UserId.>115786705183414943613< /UserId.>< Text>
The P H O here is the best in town.
We were recommended this place so we came in early before the lunch rush and there was already a wait but wasn't too long.
The interior is very vietnamese, typical tables and chairs with some wall decorations.

The menu is simple, they specialize in filet mignon  pho with thick pho noodles instead of the typical thin ones. I personally love the thick noodles because there's more texture as well as taste to it. The pho B R O T H is super duper savory and very thick in flavors.  The filet mignon is tender and juicy, thinly sliced so the meat just melts in your mouth.

The vietnamese coffee and pennywort drinks are quite delicous as well. Highly recommend this place.</Text>

A lot of people I know make the 20 minute drive from my Fullerton neighborhood to come out here because the pho is just worth it.

FOOD REVIEW
Come to a pho restaurant and you can expect their pho is going to be the best thing on the menu. Pho tai (pho filet mignon here) is my favorite and their meat portions are most likely way better than any place you've been to. Soup packs a lot of a flavor and the price is pretty reasonable as well.

It's a small restaurant, so be forewarned if you come at peak dinner times or on rainy days you'll have a bit of a wait. But their service is fast so it's not too bad< /Review><pictures>None< /pictures><resp>None<//resp><GmapID>0x80dd287d7bd4e4d9:0x6ac992fe2a792409<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<text>My review is for the taste of Pho only, regardless of the services. I don't know why this place has been highly rated. My girlfriend and I visited more than 40 Pho restaurants in both US (Southern California, Northern California, Nevada) and Vietnam but this place is the worst. The broth tasted like any regular soup base, nothing special, except for a lot of MSG used in the broth (you'll be very thirsty after eating foods that used MSG). The meats were thickly hand-cut, and hard. I am not sure the Pho noodle was fresh or not but its smell was weird. I don't recommend this place. I suggest you should instead go to Pho Holic, Kim Quy, Pho 79, Pho Vinh Ky (I and II), Pho Lu, Hoa Binh restaurant. Again, my review and my suggestions are for the taste of Pho only, not for the services. Thanks for reading.</text>< Response>

<time>1497885644680< /time>< Rate>
5</Rate>
< review>
Flew late into LAX last night and was trying to find a pho restaurant that was still opened.  Came across this place after a quick Google search & decided to give it a try.  Have to say I was pleasantly surprised! I was greeted immediately by a staff member and was seated right away.  He asked if I had children in my party and I replied yes, 1 child.  He promptly brought out a bowl of pho noodles and broth (no meat) free of charge for the child.  I think the tea is free as well.  Pho itself was tasty with a very delightful and aromatic flavor- hardly needed any hoisin/sriracha sauce. I always test the flavor of a pho by its broth and if it doesn't need much flavoring, then it passes in my book!  You have the option of big or small noodles here, I myself got the small noodles but saw many patrons got the big noodles, so maybe I'll try that next time.  The gau (fatty brisket) was pretty fatty so not a fan, but the filet mignon was pretty tender.  Egg rolls were alright and pretty pricey for just 2.  Pho prices were very good though.  The restaurant itself is small so seating can be limited.  We came in before the late night rush crowd and saw that ppl had to wait that came in after us.  SO all in all, I would return, esp since they open late on the weekends for those late night pho cravings.  Skip the egg rolls, but the pho (and price) is definitely worth it!< /review>

<rate>4<//rate><review>I order their large bowl of pho combination with thick noodle. The broth is the essence of the pho and everything else, like noodle, meat, and condiments, are their sidekicks. It's usually a good sign when pho comes out piping hot. It's just the way I prefer it especially when they insert the raw meats right before they serve. There are like four or five spices that every pho use that bring out that unique flavor in broth. My first sip of that broth I thought this wasn't pho broth. More I eat I realized the stronger essence of chicken broth over beef bone broth. It's not all that uncommon for pho places to add chicken broth later on to add more depth of their broth. I didn't mind because broth still tasted good. Within this large bowl, I experienced the most amount of meats. So much meats in fact, often times, I had to fish out for noodles and for some soup. Of course this is not a complain, I'm just stating the positive. The only down side of this pho experience was the noodle. I haven't seen that many pho places offer thick noodle so I decided to try. That was my mistake. The noodles were over cooked and quickly became even more soggier as I emptied out my bowl. I also had their spring rolls but nothing special there. I thought their peanut sauce was too thick for dipping. I would come back again and try with the usual thin pho noodles.<//review><pics>None< /pics><Resp>None< /Resp>< Gmap_id>
